#SUOMI      Operations on femoral artery with branches and connection to popliteal artery
#RUOTSI     ---
#ENGL       Operations on femoral artery with branches and connection to popliteal artery
#OHJE_S  
Deviations from Nomina Anatomica according to common usage in vascular surgery of the lower extremity: Femoral artery signifies the femoral artery proximal to the departure of the deep femoral artery.
#OHJE_R
